 Vasudev Panchal (53) has a special identity in the government high school here
 vah maathe par tikaa lagaae hue or sir ke pichley hisse main chutia baandhe dekhe jate hai

 input- IANS Lord Shiva is worshiped in Pradosh Vrat
 yah vrath hindu dharm ke sabase shubh va mahatvapurn vraton main se ek he
 According to Hindu lunar calendar, Pradosh Vrat is kept on the 13th day of the lunar month (trayodashi)
 mana jaataa he ki pradosh ke din bhagwaan shiv kii puja karne se vyakti ke paap dhul jate hai or use moksh praapt hota he
 According to the glory scriptures of Pradosha fast, keeping Pradosha fast gives the same fruits as donating two cows
 pradosh vrath ko lekar ek puranic tathy saamne aata he ki 'ek din jab chaaron or adharm kii sthiti hogi, anyaay or anachar kaa ekadhikaar hoga, manushya main swaarth bhav adhik hogi
 The person will do more of the lesser things instead of performing the act
 us samay main jo vyakti trayodashi kaa vrath rakh, shiv aradhana karegaa, us par shiv krupa hogi
 The person observing this fast moves out of the cycle of birth and moves on to the path of salvation
 use utam lok kii prapti hoti he
 The benefits of Pradosha fast are obtained according to the different Varas received from Pradosh Vrat
 - ravivaar ko padane vaale pradosh vrath se aayu vruddhi tathaa acha swasthya laabh praapt kiya ja saktaa he
 - a fast that is observed on the occasion of Trayodashi on Monday provides healing and all human desires are fulfilled
 - mangalvaar ke din trayodashi kaa pradosh vrath ho to us din ke vrath ko karne se rogon se mukti va swasthya laabh praapt hota he
 - If Pradosh is fasting on Wednesday, all the wishes of the worshiper are fulfilled
 - guuruuvaar ke din pradosh vrath pade to is din ke vrath ke fal se shatruon kaa vinaash hota he
 - Pradosh fast on Friday is done for good luck and happiness of married life
 - santan prapti kii kaamana ho to shanivaar ke din padane vaala pradosh vrath karnaa chahie
 Keeping Pradosh in view of its objectives, when the Pradosha fast is done then there is an increase in the fruits of the fast
 pradosh vrath kii vidhi- pradosh vrath karne ke liye manushya ko trayodashi ke din praat: surya udai se purv uthanaa chahie
 - After retirement, remember Lord Shri Bhole Nath
 - is vrath main aahaar nahin liya jaataa he
 - One hour before sunset after bathing all day, white clothes are worn after bathing etc
 - pujan sthal ko gangaajal yaa svachh jal se shuddh karne ke baad, gaay ke gobar se lipakar, mandap taiyaar kiya jaataa he
 - In this pavilion, Rangoli is made using five colors
 - pradosh vrath ki aradhana karne ke liye kusha ke asana kaa prayog kiya jaataa he
 In this way, after making preparations for worship, sit facing north-east direction and worship Lord Shankar
 - pujan main bhagwaan shiv ke mantra 'uun nam: shivaay' kaa jaap karte hue shiv ko jal chadhaanaa chahie

 - vrath kaa udhyapan trayodashi tithi par hi karnaa chahie
 - Lord Ganesha is worshiped a day before the festival
 purv raatri main kirthan karte hue jaagran kiya jaataa he
 - After getting up early in the morning and making a pavilion, the pavilion is prepared by decorating it with clothes and rangoli
 - 'uun uma sahit shivaay nam:' mantra kaa ek maala yani 108 baar jaap karte hue havan kiya jaataa he
 - Kheer is used for offering in havan
 - havan samaapt hone ke baad bhagwaan bholenath kii aarti kii jaati he or shaanti paath kiya jaataa he
 - In the end, two Brahmins are fed and blessed according to their capacity by giving alms
